		###########################
		## Manchu tribes unite  ###
		###########################

		country_event = {
		id = flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1322
		title = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1322.title"
		desc = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1322.desc"
		picture = chinese_general_eventPicture
		major = yes
		fire_only_once = yes


		trigger = {
		is_year = 1581
		NOT = {exists = QIN}
		NOT = {exists = MCH}
		capital_scope = {
		region = west_manchuria_region
		}
		}


		mean_time_to_happen = {        
		months = 6                                        
		}



		###########
		##options##
		###########


		option = {
		name = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1322.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }

		hidden_effect = {

		west_manchuria_region = {
		cede_province = MCH
		add_core = MCH
		add_local_autonomy = -50
		}

		east_manchuria_region = {
		add_permanent_claim = MCH
		}

		}

		}

		}





		##############################
		## Ottoman blockade of Diu ##
		##############################


		country_event = {
		id = flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1343
		title = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1343.title"
		desc = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1343.desc"
		picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
		major = yes
		fire_only_once = yes


		trigger = {
		is_year = 1538
		NOT = {is_year = 1560}
		exists = TUR
		tag = TUR
		war_with = POR
		3238 = { owned_by = POR }
		OR = {
		AND = {
		ai = yes
		war_score_against = {
		who = POR
		value = 10
		}
		}
		AND = {
		ai = no
		war_score_against = {
		who = POR
		value = 10
		}
		}
		}
		3238 = {controlled_by = TUR}

		}



		###########
		##options##
		###########


		option = {
		name = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1343.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		3238 = {
		cede_province = TUR
		}

		}

		}

		}

		##options##
		###########

		name = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1355.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		define_ruler = {
		dynasty = "de Avis"

		adm = 1
		dip = 3
		mil = 1
		name = "Henrique"
		age = 68

		}

		set_ruler_flag = temporary_regent

		add_ruler_modifier = { name = the_chaste}
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = historical_rulers_immortality } add_ruler_personality = immortal_personality }

		hidden_effect = {
		kill_heir = yes
		}

		}

		}

		## Austria asks Spain for financial aid ##

		country_event = {
		id = flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1360
		title = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1360.title"
		desc = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1360.desc"

		trigger = {
		HAB = {ai = yes}
		exists = SPA
		tag = SPA

		HAB = {is_at_war = yes}
		HAB = {num_of_loans = 3}
		is_emperor = yes
		has_ruler_modifier = "rey_emperador"
		is_year = 1516
		NOT = {has_country_modifier = family_first}
		}


		###########
		##options##
		###########


		option = {
		name = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1360.a"
		trigger = {
		OR = {
		AND = {
		ai = no
		manpower = 10
		}
		AND = {
		ai= yes
		manpower = 20
		}
		}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }

		add_treasury = -200
		add_manpower = -10

		HAB = {
		add_treasury = 200
		add_manpower = 10
		}

		add_trust = {
		who = HAB
		value = 10
		mutual = yes
		}

		hidden_effect = {
		add_country_modifier = {
		name = family_first
		duration = 3650
		}
		}


		}

		option = {
		name = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1360.b"

		OR = {
		AND = {
		ai = no
		manpower = 20
		}
		AND = {
		ai= yes
		manpower = 40
		}
		}
		}

		add_treasury = -200
		add_manpower = -20

		HAB = {
		add_treasury = 200
		add_manpower = 20
		}

		add_trust = {
		who = HAB
		value = 10
		mutual = yes
		}

		}
		}


		}

		}
		}

		add_core = SVP
		remove_core = HAB
		}
		}

		}

		#is_year = 1670

		NOT = {trade_goods = sugar}
		is_colony = no
		}
		is_subject = no
		}
		}
		has_global_flag = sugar_trade
		NOT = {has_country_flag = sugar_replantation}

		}

		##options##
		###########


		option = {
		name = "flavor_Historical_Wars_event.1504.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }


		hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = {
		which = loop
		value = 3
		}
		}

		while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = loop
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = loop
			value = 1
		}
		random_province = {
		limit = {
		NOT = { has_province_flag = replanted_sugar }
		NOT = {province_id = 481}
		NOT = {trade_goods = sugar}
		region = carribeans_region
		is_empty = no
		is_colony = no
		OR = {
		owner = {is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT}
		owned_by = ROOT
		}
		has_port = yes
		}
		change_trade_goods = sugar
		set_province_flag = replanted_sugar
		ROOT = {add_treasury = -50}
		}
		}

		}

				which = loop
				value = 1
			}
		}

			which = loop
			value = 1
		}

			which = loop

		}

			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = loop
					value = 1
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = loop
				value = 1
			}
		random_list = {
		33 = {
		AZT = {
		random_core_province = {
		spawn_rebels = {
		type = nationalist_rebels
		size = 2
		}
		}
		}
		}
		33 = {
		random_country = {
		limit = {
		is_subject_of = AZT
		}
		declare_war_with_cb = {
		who = AZT
		casus_belli = cb_independence_war
		}
		}
		}
		33 = {
		random_country = {
		limit = {
		is_neighbor_of = AZT
		OR = {
		NOT = {
		reverse_has_opinion = {
		who = AZT
		value = 0
		}
		}
		is_rival = AZT
		is_enemy = AZT
		}
		}
		declare_war_with_cb = {
		who = AZT
		casus_belli = cb_historical_wars_superiority
		}
		}
		}

		}

		}

		fire_only_once = yes


		trigger = {
		is_year = 1569
		NOT = { is_year = 1579 }
		tag = ENG
		exists = ENG
		NOT = { religion = catholic }
		ireland_region = { OR = { owned_by = ENG owner = { is_subject_of = ENG } } OR = { is_core = FTZ is_core = MNS } }
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {        
		months = 12                                        
		}
		
		
		immediate = {

		hidden_effect = {
		
		set_variable = {
			which = loop
			value = 5
		}

		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = loop
					value = 1
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = loop
				value = 1
			}
		random_province = {
		limit = {
		region = ireland_region
		OR = { owned_by = ENG owner = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
		OR = { is_core = FTZ is_core = MNS }
		}
		spawn_rebels = {
		type = nationalist_rebels
		size = 2
		}
		}
		}

		}
